<script language="javascript">
  (function() {
    var ExpireDays = 90;
    var qstr = document.location.search;
    qstr = qstr.substring(1, qstr.length);
    function SetCookie(cookieName, cookieValue, nDays) {
        var today = new Date();
        var expire = new Date();
        var maxage = 0;
        if (nDays == null || nDays == 0) nDays = 1;
        expire.setTime(today.getTime() + 3600000 * 24 * nDays);
        maxage = 3600 * 24 * nDays;
        document.cookie = cookieName + "=" + escape(cookieValue) + "; expires=" + expire.toGMTString() + "; max-age=" + maxage + "; path=/; domain=dmm.com;";
    }

    if (qstr.indexOf('sfmc_sub') != -1) {
        var thevars = qstr.split("&");
        for (var i = 0; i < thevars.length; i++) {
            var cookiecase = thevars[i].split("=");
            switch (cookiecase[0]) {
                case "sfmc_sub":
                    var sfmc_sub = cookiecase[1];
                    SetCookie("Sfmc_SubscriberID", sfmc_sub, ExpireDays);
                    break;
                case "e":
                    var e = cookiecase[1];
                    SetCookie("Sfmc_EmailAddr_", e, ExpireDays);
                    break;
                case "j":
                    var j = cookiecase[1];
                    SetCookie("Sfmc_JobID", j, ExpireDays);
                    break;
                case "l":
                    var l = cookiecase[1];
                    SetCookie("Sfmc_ListID", l, ExpireDays);
                    break;
                case "jb":
                    var jb = cookiecase[1];
                    SetCookie("Sfmc_BatchID", jb, ExpireDays);
                    break;
                case "u":
                    var u = cookiecase[1];
                    SetCookie("Sfmc_UrlID", u, ExpireDays);
                    break;
                case "mid":
                    var mid = cookiecase[1];
                    SetCookie("Sfmc_MemberID", mid, ExpireDays);
                    break;
                default:
                    break;
            }
        }
    }
  })();
</script>

<script>

$('#fn-rotate').setRotateBnr();
var adserverCarousel = new AdserverCarousel();

var i3SegmentBanners = JSON.parse('{"bannerType":"cx","segmentCode":"default","bannerId":"","adProductId":"","clickUrl":"","imageUrl":""}');
var linkUrl = i3SegmentBanners["clickUrl"];
var adProductId = i3SegmentBanners["adProductId"];
var i3AdSpaceIndex = 0;

$(function()
{
    //バックフィルバナーをセット
    adserverCarousel.backfillBanners = JSON.parse('[{"image":"\/\/p.dmm.com\/p\/bnr\/ad\/rotation\/rental01_g.jpg","url":"http:\/\/ad.dmm.com\/ad\/p\/r?_site=242&_article=9743&_link=251218&_image=251305","alt":"","target":""},{"image":"\/\/p.dmm.com\/p\/bnr\/ad\/rotation\/book01_g.jpg","url":"http:\/\/ad.dmm.com\/ad\/p\/r?_site=242&_article=9743&_link=258292&_image=258382","alt":"","target":""},{"image":"\/\/p.dmm.com\/p\/bnr\/ad\/rotation\/netgame01_g.jpg","url":"http:\/\/ad.dmm.com\/ad\/p\/r?_site=242&_article=9743&_link=258293&_image=258383","alt":"","target":""},{"image":"\/\/p.dmm.com\/p\/bnr\/ad\/rotation\/make01_g.jpg","url":"http:\/\/ad.dmm.com\/ad\/p\/r?_site=242&_article=9743&_link=258291&_image=258381","alt":"","target":""},{"image":"\/\/p.dmm.com\/p\/bnr\/ad\/center\/slider_center_01_g.jpg","url":"http:\/\/ad.dmm.com\/ad\/p\/r?_site=242&_article=9743&_link=196995&_image=197079","alt":"","target":""}]');

    //アドサーバから広告を取得できない場合代替広告を設置
    setTimeout("adserverCarousel.insertAlternateAd(i3SegmentBanners)", 5000);
});

var renderCarouselAndRectangleAd = function(data, context){
    if (data && data.searchResult && data.searchResult.spaces) {
        var adspaces = data.searchResult.spaces;
        for (var adspaceIdx = 0; adspaceIdx < adspaces.length; adspaceIdx++) {
            var ads = adspaces[adspaceIdx].ads;
            if(adspaces[adspaceIdx].id === '00000001636975f1'){
                 renderCarouselAd(ads);
            }else if(adspaces[adspaceIdx].id === '000000015fcc2101'){
                 renderRightAd(ads);
            }
        }
    }
}

//広告配信サーバへのリクエスト送信に対するコールバック関数
var renderCarouselAd = function(data, context) {
    if(data){
        //広告スペースが存在する場合は広告オブジェクトを取得
        var ads = data;

        //商品IDからセットするカルーセルバナーの位置を取得
        adsCount = ads.length;
        for(var i = 0; i < adsCount; i++){
            if(ads[i]["product"] == adProductId){
                i3AdSpaceIndex = i;
                break;
            }
        }

        if("cx" == "i3"){
            //i3セグメントバナーで配信
            if(ads[i3AdSpaceIndex].creative.images && ads[i3AdSpaceIndex].creative.images[0]){
                //コンボクリエイティブの場合
                ads[i3AdSpaceIndex]["clickUrl"] = linkUrl;
                ads[i3AdSpaceIndex]["creative"]["images"][0]["source"] = i3SegmentBanners["imageUrl"];
            }else{
                //イメージクリエイティブの場合
                ads[i3AdSpaceIndex]["clickUrl"] = linkUrl;
                ads[i3AdSpaceIndex]["creative"]["source"] = i3SegmentBanners["imageUrl"];
            }
        }else{
            //アドサーババナーで配信
            linkUrl = ads[i3AdSpaceIndex]["clickUrl"];
        }
        //i3セグメントバナーにi3クリックイベントを仕込む
        var carouselIndex = "carousel" + (i3AdSpaceIndex + 1);
        $("ul.m-rotate__mainList li.m-rotate__mainListItem").find("." + carouselIndex).on("click", clickBanner);

        if (ads.length > 0) {
            adserverCarousel.setBanners(ads);
        }

        adserverCarousel.finalize();
    }
}

//PC総合トップ i3 Tag Start
i3('create', 'carouselBanner');
var bannerType = i3SegmentBanners["bannerType"];
var segmentCode = i3SegmentBanners["segmentCode"];
var bannerId = i3SegmentBanners["bannerId"];
var contentId = bannerId ? bannerType + '-' + segmentCode + "-" + bannerId : bannerType + '-' + segmentCode;

i3('carouselBanner.add', 'banner', {content_id: contentId});

// 送信
i3('carouselBanner.send', 'show', 'banner');

function clickBanner(event) {
    // クリックされたアイテムの情報
    i3("create", "carouselBanner");
    i3("carouselBanner.set", "detail", {
        via_info: "banner", //固定
        vir_option: "general.top.carousel",
        via_view_rank: 1 // バナー枠内での表示順
    });
    i3("carouselBanner.add", "detail", {
        content_id: contentId
    });
    // ログの送信
    i3("carouselBanner.send", "click", "banner");
}
//総合トップ i3 Tag End

</script>

<script>
    function isValidBrowser() {
        var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
        if (ua.indexOf("Trident") >= 0) {
            //IE
            var ieVersion = window.navigator.appVersion.match(/MSIE (\d+)/);
            if (ieVersion == null) {
                //IE11
                return true;
            } else if (typeof(ieVersion) && ieVersion[1] == "10") {
                //IE10
                return true;
            }
        } else {
            //IE以外
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }
    if (isValidBrowser()) {
        //アドテクライブラリを動的に呼びだし
        var scriptEl = document.createElement('script');
        scriptEl.type = 'text/javascript';
        scriptEl.async = 'async';
        scriptEl.src = "/js/adtech/mkbase/displayad.js";
        var targetEl = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
        targetEl.parentNode.insertBefore(scriptEl, targetEl);
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
//広告設置済みの場合true, 未設置の場合false
var isRightAd = false;
var isRightSpecialVideoAd1 = false;
var isRightSpecialVideoAd2 = false;
var adVideoProductSP1Id = "0000000163eab669";
var adVideoProductSP2Id = "0000000163efd79e";

//JS 内で利用するPHPの値をオブジェクトに格納
var phpParam = {
    "isDev" : "",
    "isAdult" : "",
    "normalSpaceId" : "000000015fcc2101"
};


$(function(){
    //遅らせてレンダリング関数を実行する
    setTimeout(insertAlternateRightAd, 5000);
    setTimeout(insertAlternateRightSpecialVideoAd, 5000);
});

function createRightBanner(ad)
{
    var img = document.createElement("img");
    var link = document.createElement("a");
    link.href = ad.clickUrl;

    if (ad.creative.images && ad.creative.images[0]) {
        //コンボクリエイティブの場合
        if (ad.creative.content) {
            for (contentIndex in ad.creative.content) {
                //オプションが設定されている場合
                switch (ad.creative.content[contentIndex].key) {
                case "target":
                    //管理画面でtargetの値を登録しないとcontent属性値が空配列になることに注意！
                    link.target = ad.creative.content[contentIndex].value;
                    break;
                case "説明":
                    //説明が登録されていたら代替テキストをセット
                    img.alt = ad.creative.content[contentIndex].value;
                    break;
                default:
                }
            }
        }

        img.src = ad.creative.images[0].source;
    } else {
        //イメージクリエイティブの場合
        img.src = ad.creative.source;

        if (ad.creative.description) {
            //説明が登録されていたら代替テキストをセット
            img.alt = ad.creative.description;
        }
    }

    link.style.margin = "0px 3px 12px 3px";
    link.style.display = "block";
    link.appendChild(img);
    return link;
}
//レクタングル枠のバナー
var rectangleAdCallBackAds;
//リクエスト元のアドサーバタグはSP総合TOPのカルーセル枠
//広告配信サーバへのリクエスト送信に対するコールバック関数
function renderRightAd(ads, context) {
    if (isRightAd) return;
    if(ads) {
        rectangleAdCallBackAds = ads;

        //動画広告のタイトルを取得して配列形式でリクエストパラメータに渡す
        var adRequestKeyword;
        adRequestKeyword = getAdserverVideoTitle(ads);

        //動画フッターバナーへのコールバック関数内でレクタングル枠のバナーをレンダリング
        cX.callQueue.push(['insertAdSpace', {
            adSpaceId: '0000000163efcf09',
            baseAdDeliveryUrl: 'http://display.dmm.com/adserver/search',
            secureBaseAdDeliveryUrl: 'https://display.dmm.com/adserver/search',
            sz: '244×165',
            k: adRequestKeyword,
            renderFunction: getNVBannerAndRectangleRender
        }]);
    }else{
        //登録バナーが足りないときやアドサーバ側のバグによって意図する広告を取得できなかった場合
        insertAlternateRightAd();
    }
}
//アドサーバのレスポンス結果からビデオクリエイティブのタイトルを配列形式で抽出
function getAdserverVideoTitle(ads){
    var videoTitles = [];
    if (ads) {
        ads.forEach(function (ad) {
            if (ad.creative.videoFiles && ad.creative.templateName.indexOf("standard-video") != -1) {
                videoTitles.push(ad.creative.title.trim());
            }
        })
    }
    return videoTitles;
}
//動画フッターバナー枠へリクエストを投げてから、レクタングル通常枠レンダリング
function getNVBannerAndRectangleRender(data, context){

    // レクタングル動画付属枠 のアドスペースIDを取得
    var footerAdSpaceId= data.searchResult.spaces[0].id;

    // 動画付属枠取得の関数内で通常枠の取得を行なっている
    // レクタングル通常枠 のアドスペースIDを保持しておく。
    var normalAdSpaceId = phpParam.normalSpaceId;

    if (data && data.searchResult && data.searchResult.spaces && data.searchResult.spaces[0] && data.searchResult.spaces[0].ads) {
        rectangleCM.setRectangleNormalBanner(data.searchResult.spaces[0].ads);
    } else {
        //動画フッターバナーを取得できなかった場合
    }
    //動画フッターバナーの取得結果を問わずレンダリング開始
    var ads = rectangleAdCallBackAds;

    //レクタングル通常枠の動画広告のデータセットを作成
    rectangleCM.createRectangleNormalMovie(ads, normalAdSpaceId, footerAdSpaceId);

    var adCount = 0;
    if (rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"]["nv-1"]) {
        //通常レクタングル枠①への動画広告レンダリング
        $("#right-ad-container").append(createRectangleVideoDOM(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"], "nv-1"));
        setEventCM("nv-1");
        adCount++;
    }
    if (rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"]["nv-2"]) {
        //通常レクタングル枠②への動画広告レンダリング
        $("#right-ad-container").append(createRectangleVideoDOM(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"], "nv-2"));
        setEventCM("nv-2");
        adCount++;
    }
    //通常枠の配信クリエイティブ上限
    if(adCount === 2){
        isRightAd = true;
        return;
    }
    //動画広告のレンダリング後に画像バナーをレンダリング
    ads.forEach(function(ad) {
        //動画広告用のバナー画像を省いてレンダリング
        var adLinks = null;
        if (adCount < 2) {
            if (ad.creative.images && ad.creative.images[0]) {
                //通常枠の'a'タグを作成する。(必要な属性を付与する)
                //コンボクリエイティブの場合
                if(ad.creative.images.length === 1) {
                    var adLink = createRightBanner(ad);
                    adLink.dataset.adgroupId = ad.id;
                    adLink.dataset.bannerCategory = "newtab";
                    adLink.dataset.order = adCount + 1;
                    adLink.dataset.adspaceName = "rectangle_standard";
                    adLink.dataset.adspaceId = normalAdSpaceId;
                    mousedownForTracking(adLink);
                    document.querySelector("#right-ad-container").appendChild(adLink);
                    adCount++;
                }else{
                    //動画広告用のコンボクリエイティブは描画しない ad.creative.images.length が 2か3
                }
            }else{
                if(!ad.creative.videoFiles){
                    //通常枠の'a'タグを作成する。(必要な属性を付与する)
                    //イメージクリエイティブの場合
                    var adLink = createRightBanner(ad);
                    adLink.dataset.adgroupId = ad.id;
                    adLink.dataset.bannerCategory = "regular";
                    adLink.dataset.order = adCount + 1;
                    adLink.dataset.adspaceName = "rectangle_standard";
                    adLink.dataset.adspaceId = normalAdSpaceId;
                    mousedownForTracking(adLink);
                    document.querySelector("#right-ad-container").appendChild(adLink);
                    adCount++;
                }
            }
        }else{
            //動画広告用のバナーは最低でも画像2枚のコンボクリエイティブ
            isRightAd = true;
            return;
        }
    });
}
var videoFrameIndexSP = 1;
function renderSpecialRectangleVideoAd(data, context){
    var adFrame;
    if (data && data.searchResult && data.searchResult.spaces && data.searchResult.spaces[0] && data.searchResult.spaces[0].ads) {
        var ads = data.searchResult.spaces[0].ads;
        var spaceId = data.searchResult.spaces[0].id;
        if(ads[0].product === adVideoProductSP1Id){
            adFrame = "sv-1";
        }else if(ads[0].product === adVideoProductSP2Id){
            adFrame = "sv-2";
        }else{
            //広告商品IDの設定が間違っている場合でも、リクエスト順番に描画
            $("#video-sv-1").length === 0 ? adFrame = "sv-1" : adFrame = "sv-2";
        }

        //CM特別枠のCMの作成
        rectangleCM.createRectangleCmMovie(ads, adFrame, spaceId);
        rectangleCM.setRectangleCmBanner(ads, adFrame);
    } else {
        //リクエスト失敗時は何もしない
    }
    if (rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adFrame]) {
        //CM特別動画枠①②の順に配置
        if(adFrame == "sv-1"){
            if(rectangleCM.checkRectangleCmMovieFormat(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adFrame]) && (rectangleCM["sv-1_LENGTH"] === rectangleCM["sv-1-banner-count"] || rectangleCM["sv-1-banner-count"] === "ALL")){
                isRightSpecialVideoAd1 = true;
                if ($("#movie-sv-1").length === 0) {
                    //特別枠を作成する。第３引数には、付属バナーにセットする広告スペースIDを入れる
                    //特別枠の場合、付属バナー用の広告スペースを作成していないので,付属バナーにも特別枠の広告スペースIDをセットする
                    $("#right-ad-container").prepend(createRectangleVideoDOM(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"], adFrame));
                    setEventCM(adFrame);
                }
            }else{
                //バックフィルバナーフラグ
                isRightSpecialVideoAd1 = false;
            }
        }else if(adFrame == "sv-2"){
            if(rectangleCM.checkRectangleCmMovieFormat(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adFrame]) && (rectangleCM["sv-2_LENGTH"] === rectangleCM["sv-2-banner-count"] || rectangleCM["sv-2-banner-count"] === "ALL")) {
                isRightSpecialVideoAd2 = true;
                if ($("#movie-sv-2").length === 0) {
                    if ($("#video-sv-1-0").length === 0) {
                        //特別枠を作成する。第３引数には、付属バナーにセットする広告スペースIDを入れる
                        //特別枠の場合、付属バナー用の広告スペースを作成していないので,付属バナーにも特別枠の広告スペースIDをセットする
                        $("#right-ad-container").prepend(createRectangleVideoDOM(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"], adFrame));
                    } else {
                        //特別枠を作成する。第３引数には、付属バナーにセットする広告スペースIDを入れる
                        //特別枠の場合、付属バナー用の広告スペースを作成していないので,付属バナーにも特別枠の広告スペースIDをセットする
                        $("#right-ad-container").children().eq(0).after(createRectangleVideoDOM(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"], adFrame));
                    }
                    setEventCM(adFrame);
                }
            }else{
                //バックフィルバナーフラグ
                isRightSpecialVideoAd2 = false;
            }
        }
    }
    videoFrameIndexSP++;
}
var rectangleCM = {
    //MOVIE_DATA：動画広告のハッシュ  BACKFILL_MOVIE_DATA：バックフィル動画広告のハッシュ
    "MOVIE_DATA" : {}, "BACKFILL_MOVIE_DATA" : {},
    //sv:レクタングル動画特別枠  nv:レクタングル通常枠
    "sv-1_videoIndex" : 0, "sv-2_videoIndex" : 0, "sv-1_LENGTH" : 0, "sv-2_LENGTH" : 0, "sv-1-banner-count":0, "sv-2-banner-count":0, "nv-banner-count":0,
    /**
     *
     * @param ads アドサーバのCMデータの返却値
     * @param adframe 枠の名前
     * @param spaceId 広告スペースID
     */
    createRectangleCmMovie : function(ads, adframe, spaceId){
        var videoTemplateType = "cm-video";
        var bannerCount = 0;

        //ビデオデータのみの配列
        var rectangleVideoOnlyDataList = [];
        var rectangleCmData = [];
        ads.forEach(function(ad){
            rectangleCmData = [];
            if(ad.creative.videoFiles && ad.creative.templateName.indexOf(videoTemplateType) != -1){
                //アンカー に持たせる独自要素を入れる
                rectangleCmData['spaceId'] = spaceId;
                rectangleCmData['spaceName'] = adframe === "sv-1" ? "rectangle_special1":"rectangle_special2";
                rectangleCmData['groupId'] = ad.id;
                rectangleCmData['videoTitle'] = ad.creative.title;
                rectangleCmData['videoBanner'] = ad.creative.videoFiles[0].source;
                rectangleCmData['clickUrl'] = ad.clickUrl;
                rectangleCmData['rectangleCmTemplate'] = ad.creative.templateName;
                rectangleVideoOnlyDataList.push(rectangleCmData);
            }else if(ad.creative.templateName === "cm-video-combo"){
                if(ad.creative.title[0].indexOf("-ALL") == -1) {
                    ad.creative.images.forEach(function (comboImage) {
                        if (comboImage.key.indexOf("-footer-default-img") != -1) {
                            bannerCount++;
                        }
                    });
                }else{
                    bannerCount = "ALL";
                }
            }
        });

        if(rectangleVideoOnlyDataList.length === 0) return;
        rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adframe] = rectangleVideoOnlyDataList;
        rectangleCM[adframe + "-banner-count"] = bannerCount;
        rectangleCM[adframe + "_LENGTH"] = rectangleVideoOnlyDataList.length;
    },
    setRectangleCmBanner : function(ads, adframe){
        //取得した動画クリエイティブに対応するバナーをコンボクリエイティブからセット
        var videoCount = rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe].length;
        for(var i = 0;i < videoCount;i++){
            var rectangleCmTemplate
            if(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][i].videoTitle.match(/cm[0-9]{1}\-/)){
                rectangleCmTemplate = "cm-video" + rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][i].videoTitle.slice(2, 3);
            }else{
                rectangleCmTemplate = "cm-video" + rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][i].videoTitle.slice(2, 4);
            }
            rectangleCM.relateCmVideoAndBanner(ads, adframe, rectangleCmTemplate,i);
            ads.forEach(function(ad) {
                if (ad.creative.title[0].slice(-4) === "-ALL") {
                    //対応する付属バナーがない動画は、cm1でALLの名前が設定されている付属バナーをセット
                    if(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][i]) {
                        if (!rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][i].cmBanner) {
                            rectangleCmTemplate = "cm-video1";
                            rectangleCM.relateCmVideoAndBanner(ads, adframe, rectangleCmTemplate, i);
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    },
    relateCmVideoAndBanner : function(ads, adframe, rectangleCmTemplate, videoindex){
        var creativeTitle;
        if(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].videoTitle.match(/cm[0-9]{1}\-/)){
            creativeTitle = rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].videoTitle.slice(4);
        }else{
            //※cmXX-*****の*****を切り取る
            creativeTitle = rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].videoTitle.slice(5);
        }
        var videoTemplateType = rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].rectangleCmTemplate;

        ads.forEach(function(adData) {
            if (adData.creative.images && adData.creative.templateName.indexOf(videoTemplateType) != -1) {
                //コンボクリエイティブの名前と動画クリエイティブの名前が一致するものだけペアを作成
                if(adData.creative.title[0] === creativeTitle){
                    adData.creative.images.forEach(function (cmAdBanner) {
                        if (cmAdBanner.key === rectangleCmTemplate + "-footer-default-img") {
                            rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].cmBanner = cmAdBanner.source;
                        } else if (cmAdBanner.key === rectangleCmTemplate + "-footer-hover-img") {
                            rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].onMouseBanner = cmAdBanner.source;
                        } else if (cmAdBanner.key === rectangleCmTemplate + "-end-img") {
                            rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].posterBanner = cmAdBanner.source;
                        }
                    });
                    //コンボクリエイティブに設定したtargetとaltを取得
                    if (adData.creative.content) {
                        adData.creative.content.forEach(function (adCon) {
                            if (adCon.key === "cm-video-target") {
                                rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].target = adCon.value;
                            } else if (adCon.key === "cm-video-alt") {
                                rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].alt = adCon.value;
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    if (!rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].posterBanner) rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].posterBanner = "";
                    if (!rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].onMouseBanner) rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].onMouseBanner = rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].cmBanner;
                    if (!rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].target) rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].target = "";
                    if (!rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].alt) rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoindex].alt = "";
                }
            }
        });
    },
    checkRectangleCmMovieFormat : function(rectangleCmData){
        var cmVideoCount = rectangleCmData.length;
        for(var i = 0;i < cmVideoCount; i++){
            if(!rectangleCmData[i].videoBanner)  return false;
            if(!rectangleCmData[i].clickUrl)     return false;
            if(!rectangleCmData[i].cmBanner)  return false;
        }
        return true;
    },
    createRectangleNormalMovie : function(ads,adSpaceId, footerAdSpaceId){
        var adBannerIndex;
        var rectangleBannerData = [];
        var adframeIndex = 1;
        //動画と付属バナーのセットの作成フラグ
        var videoAndCmBannerPair;
        //adsはレクタングル枠のクリエイティブ
        ads.some(function (ad) {
            if (ad.creative.videoFiles && ad.creative.templateName.indexOf("standard-video") != -1) {
                for(i = 1; i < rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA["nv-banner-count"]; i++){
                    videoAndCmBannerPair = false;
                    adBannerIndex = "nv-banner-" + i;
                    rectangleBannerData = [];
                    if (rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adBannerIndex]['videoTitle'] === ad.creative.title.trim()) {
                        rectangleBannerData['groupId'] = ad.id;
                        rectangleBannerData['adSpaceId'] = adSpaceId;
                        rectangleBannerData['footerAdSpaceId'] = footerAdSpaceId;
                        rectangleBannerData['videoTitle'] = rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adBannerIndex]['videoTitle'];
                        rectangleBannerData['cmBanner'] = rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adBannerIndex]['cmBanner'];
                        rectangleBannerData['onMouseBanner'] = rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adBannerIndex]['onMouseBanner'];
                        rectangleBannerData['posterBanner'] = rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adBannerIndex]['posterBanner'];
                        rectangleBannerData['target'] = rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adBannerIndex]['target'];
                        rectangleBannerData['alt'] = rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adBannerIndex]['alt'];
                        rectangleBannerData['videoBanner'] = ad.creative.videoFiles[0].source;
                        rectangleBannerData['clickUrl'] = ad.clickUrl;
                        rectangleBannerData['nvBannerClickUrl'] = rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adBannerIndex]['nvBannerClickUrl'];
                        rectangleBannerData['rectangleCmTemplate'] = ad.creative.templateName;
                        //オンマウスバナーは任意設定項目
                        if (!rectangleBannerData['onMouseBanner']) rectangleBannerData['onMouseBanner'] = rectangleBannerData["cmBanner"];
                        if (!rectangleBannerData['posterBanner']) rectangleBannerData['posterBanner'] = "";
                        if (!rectangleBannerData['target']) rectangleBannerData['target'] = "";
                        if (!rectangleBannerData['alt']) rectangleBannerData['alt'] = "";
                        //動画広告のセットを確認して追加
                        if (rectangleCM.checkRectangleMovieData(rectangleBannerData)) {
                            //通常枠の動画広告
                            adframe = "nv-" + adframeIndex;
                            rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adframe] = rectangleBannerData;
                            adframeIndex++;
                            videoAndCmBannerPair = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
                //対応する付属バナーを取得できなかった動画
                if(!videoAndCmBannerPair) {
                    rectangleBannerData = [];
                    rectangleBannerData['groupId'] = ad.id;
                    rectangleBannerData['adSpaceId'] = adSpaceId;
                    rectangleBannerData['videoBanner'] = ad.creative.videoFiles[0].source;
                    rectangleBannerData['clickUrl'] = ad.clickUrl;
                    rectangleBannerData['rectangleCmTemplate'] = ad.creative.templateName;
                    //動画広告のセットを確認して追加
                    if (rectangleCM.checkRectangleMovieData(rectangleBannerData)) {
                        //通常枠の動画広告
                        adframe = "nv-" + adframeIndex;
                        rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adframe] = rectangleBannerData;
                        adframeIndex++;
                    }
                    //通常枠は動画クリエイティブは2つまで
                    if(adframeIndex > 2){return;}
                }
            }
        });
    },
    setRectangleNormalBanner : function(normalCmBannerAds){
        //通常枠の動画広告のバナーをセット
        var normalCmBannerData = [];
        var normalCmBannerTemplateName = "standard-video";
        var nmVideoIndex = 1;
        normalCmBannerAds.forEach(function(ad){
            normalCmBannerData = [];
            if(ad.creative.images && ad.creative.templateName.indexOf(normalCmBannerTemplateName) != -1){
                normalCmBannerData['nvBannerClickUrl'] = ad.clickUrl;
                normalCmBannerData['videoTitle'] = ad.creative.title.toString().trim();
                ad.creative.images.forEach(function(cmAdBanner){
                    if (cmAdBanner.key === normalCmBannerTemplateName + "-footer-default-img") {
                        normalCmBannerData['cmBanner'] = cmAdBanner.source;
                    } else if (cmAdBanner.key === normalCmBannerTemplateName + "-footer-hover-img") {
                        normalCmBannerData['onMouseBanner'] = cmAdBanner.source;
                    } else if (cmAdBanner.key === normalCmBannerTemplateName + "-end-img") {
                        normalCmBannerData['posterBanner'] = cmAdBanner.source;
                    }
                });
                if (ad.creative.content) {
                    ad.creative.content.forEach(function (adCon) {
                        if (adCon.key === normalCmBannerTemplateName + "-target") {
                            normalCmBannerData['target'] = adCon.value[0];
                        } else if (adCon.key === normalCmBannerTemplateName + "-alt") {
                            normalCmBannerData['alt'] = adCon.value[0];
                        }
                    });
                }
                if (!normalCmBannerData['target']) normalCmBannerData['target'] = "";
                if (!normalCmBannerData['alt']) normalCmBannerData['alt'] = "";
                if(normalCmBannerData["videoTitle"]){
                    rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA["nv-banner-" + nmVideoIndex] = normalCmBannerData;
                    nmVideoIndex++;
                }
            }
        });
        rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA["nv-banner-count"] = nmVideoIndex;
    },
    checkRectangleMovieData : function(rectangleCmData){
        if(!rectangleCmData["videoBanner"])  return false;
        if(!rectangleCmData["clickUrl"])     return false;
        if(!rectangleCmData["cmBanner"] && rectangleCmData["posterBanner"]) return false;
        return true;
    },
    createRectangleCmBackFillMovie : function(rectangleBackfillCm, adframeType){
        var iniFirstIndex = 0;
        adframeType == "sv-1" ? iniFirstIndex = 0: iniFirstIndex = 3;

        var rectangleCms = [];
        var rectangleVideoData = [];
        for(i = iniFirstIndex; i < iniFirstIndex + 3; i++){
            rectangleVideoData = [];
            if(rectangleBackfillCm[i]){
                //バックフィルの属性を加える
                rectangleVideoData["spaceId"] = "0";
                rectangleVideoData["groupId"] = "0";
                rectangleVideoData['spaceName'] = adframeType === "sv-1" ? "rectangle_special1":"rectangle_special2";
                rectangleVideoData["videoTitle"] = rectangleBackfillCm[i]["videoTitle"];
                rectangleVideoData["videoBanner"] = rectangleBackfillCm[i]["videoBanner"];
                rectangleVideoData["clickUrl"] = rectangleBackfillCm[i]["clickUrl"];
                rectangleVideoData["rectangleCmTemplate"] = rectangleBackfillCm[i]["rectangleCmTemplate"];
                rectangleVideoData["cmBanner"] = rectangleBackfillCm[i]["cmBanner"];
                rectangleVideoData["onMouseBanner"] = rectangleBackfillCm[i]["onMouseBanner"];
                rectangleVideoData["posterBanner"] = rectangleBackfillCm[i]["posterBanner"];
                rectangleVideoData["target"] = rectangleBackfillCm[i]["target"];
                rectangleVideoData["alt"] = rectangleBackfillCm[i]["alt"];
                if(rectangleCM.checkRectangleMovieData(rectangleVideoData)){
                    if (!rectangleVideoData['onMouseBanner']) rectangleVideoData['onMouseBanner'] = rectangleVideoData["cmBanner"];
                    if (!rectangleVideoData['target']) rectangleVideoData['target'] = "";
                    if (!rectangleVideoData['alt']) rectangleVideoData['alt'] = "";
                    rectangleCms.push(rectangleVideoData);
                }
            }
        }
        if(rectangleCms.length === 0) return;
        rectangleCM.MOVIE_DATA[adframeType] = rectangleCms;
        rectangleCM[adframeType + "_LENGTH"] = rectangleCms.length;
    }
};

//初回videoタグ設置時にバインド
function setEventCM(adframe){
    var videoCmTag;
    var videoEventIndex = rectangleCM[adframe+"_videoIndex"];
    var videoData = [];
    var videoplayTag = $('#top-cm-div-token-'+ adframe);
    var videoBlankPoster = "//p.dmm.com/p/top/bnr/transparent.png";
    if(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][0]){
        videoData = rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][0];
    }else{
        videoData = rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe];
    }
    if(adframe === "sv-1"|| adframe === "sv-2"){
        var videoCount = rectangleCM[adframe + "_LENGTH"];
        //生成するvideoタグは1枠につき最大2つ
        for(i = 0; i < videoCount; i++){
            videoCmTag = $('#video-'+ adframe + "-" + i);
            if(i == 0) {
                videoCmTag.one('canplaythrough', function () {
                    //再生準備完了まで止め画像を表示
                    videoplayTag.css('visibility', 'hidden');
                    videoCmTag.css('visibility', '');
                });
            }
            videoCmTag.get(0).addEventListener("ended", function() {
                endNextCM(adframe);
            });
            videoCmTag.get(0).muted = true;
            if(i == 1) break;
        }
        videoCmTag = $('#video-'+ adframe + "-0");
        videoCmTag.css('visibility', 'hidden');
        videoCmTag.show();
        videoCmTag.get(0).play();
        if(ua.indexOf('msie') != -1 || ua.indexOf('trident') != -1) {
            videoCmTag.get(0).poster = videoBlankPoster;
            videoCmTag.get(0).load();
        }else{
            videoCmTag.get(0).poster = videoData.posterBanner ? videoData.posterBanner : "";
        }
    }else if(adframe === "nv-1"|| adframe === "nv-2"){
        if(!videoData.cmBanner){
            //フッターバナーなしでも再生
            videoplayTag.height(138).width(244);
        }
        videoCmTag = $('#video-'+ adframe);
        videoCmTag.get(0).addEventListener("ended", function() {
            endNextCM(adframe);
        });
        videoCmTag.one('canplaythrough', function () {
            //再生準備完了まで止め画像を表示
            videoplayTag.css('visibility', 'hidden');
            videoCmTag.css('visibility', '');
        });
        videoCmTag.css('visibility', 'hidden');
        videoCmTag.get(0).muted = true;
        videoCmTag.get(0).play();
        if(ua.indexOf('msie') != -1 || ua.indexOf('trident') != -1) {
            videoCmTag.get(0).poster = videoBlankPoster;
            videoCmTag.get(0).load();
        }else{
            videoCmTag.get(0).poster = videoData.posterBanner ? videoData.posterBanner : "";
        }
    }

    var videoBannerTag = $('#cm-banner-'+ adframe);
    videoBannerTag.hover(
        function(){
            if(adframe == "sv-1"){
                videoEventIndex = rectangleCM["sv-1_videoIndex"];
                $(this).find('img').attr('src',rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].onMouseBanner);
            }else if(adframe == "sv-2"){
                videoEventIndex = rectangleCM["sv-2_videoIndex"];
                $(this).find('img').attr('src',rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].onMouseBanner);
            }else if(adframe == "nv-1" || adframe == "nv-2"){
                $(this).find('img').attr('src',videoData.onMouseBanner);
            }
        },
        function(){
            if(adframe == "sv-1"){
                videoEventIndex = rectangleCM["sv-1_videoIndex"];
                $(this).find('img').attr('src',rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].cmBanner);
            }else if(adframe == "sv-2"){
                videoEventIndex = rectangleCM["sv-2_videoIndex"];
                $(this).find('img').attr('src',rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].cmBanner);
            }else if(adframe == "nv-1" || adframe == "nv-2"){
                $(this).find('img').attr('src',videoData.cmBanner);
            }
        }
    );
}

function endNextCM(adframe){
    //再生中のvideoタグと次再生videoタグ
    var videoActiveTag;
    var videoNextTag;

    //再生したい動画ソースのindex
    var videoEventIndex;

    var videoPlayTagIndex;
    var videoNextPlayTagIndex;
    if(adframe === "sv-1" || adframe === "sv-2"){
        videoEventIndex = rectangleCM[adframe + "_videoIndex"];
        if(rectangleCM[adframe + "_LENGTH"] > 1){
            videoPlayTagIndex = $('#video-' + adframe + "-0").is(':visible') ? 0 : 1;
        }else{
            //動画素材の数が1つの場合はvideoタグは1つしかない
            videoPlayTagIndex = 0;
        }
        videoNextPlayTagIndex = 1 - videoPlayTagIndex;
        videoActiveTag = $('#video-' + adframe + "-" + videoPlayTagIndex);
    }else if(adframe === "nv-1" || adframe === "nv-2") {
        videoEventIndex = 0;
        videoActiveTag = $('#video-' + adframe);
    }
    var videoLink = $('#movie-' + adframe);
    var cmBanner = $('#cm-banner-' + adframe);
    var cmSound = $('#cm-sound-token_' + adframe);
    var videoBlankPoster = "//p.dmm.com/p/top/bnr/transparent.png";

    var listenerKey = null;
    var loadedDef = null;
    var posterDisplay = false;
    $.when(
        function(){
            loadedDef = new $.Deferred();
            if(adframe === "sv-1" || adframe === "sv-2"){
                if(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].posterBanner) {
                    posterDisplay = true;
                }
                videoActiveTag.removeClass('is-play');
                cmBanner.css('visibility', 'hidden');
                cmSound.css('visibility', 'hidden');
                videoActiveTag.height(165).width(244);

                if(posterDisplay) {
                    videoActiveTag.get(0).poster = rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].posterBanner ? rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].posterBanner : videoBlankPoster;
                    videoActiveTag.get(0).load();
                }
                rectangleCM[adframe +"_videoIndex"]++;
                if(rectangleCM[adframe + "_videoIndex"] > rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe].length - 1) {rectangleCM[adframe + "_videoIndex"] = 0};
                videoEventIndex = rectangleCM[adframe + "_videoIndex"];
                if(rectangleCM[adframe + "_LENGTH"] > 1) {
                    videoNextTag = $('#video-' + adframe + "-" + videoNextPlayTagIndex);
                    videoNextTag.get(0).load();
                }else{
                	//動画素材の数が1つの場合、再生対象のvideoタグは常に同一
                    videoNextTag = videoActiveTag;
                }
                listenerKey = videoNextTag.get(0).addEventListener('canplay', function() {
                    if(loadedDef) {
                        loadedDef.resolve();
                        loadedDef = null;
                    }
                });
                //止め画像なしの動画広告 → 次の動画再生
                if(!posterDisplay) {
                    videoNextTag.get(0).poster = videoBlankPoster;
                    videoNextTag.get(0).load();
                    videoNextTag.one('canplay', function(){
                        videoActiveTag.hide();
                        videoNextTag.get(0).play();
                        videoLink.find("a").attr("target",rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].target);
                        videoLink.find("a").attr("alt",rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].alt);
                        videoLink.find("a").attr("href",rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].clickUrl);
                        cmBanner.find("img").attr('src', rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].cmBanner);
                        cmBanner.find("a").attr('href', rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].clickUrl);
                        if((ua.indexOf('safari')  !== -1 && ua.indexOf('chrome') === -1))
                        {
                            videoNextTag.fadeIn('slow');
                        }else{
                            videoNextTag.show();
                        }
                        var videoLoadIndex = videoEventIndex + 1 > rectangleCM[adframe + "_LENGTH"] - 1 ? 0  : videoEventIndex + 1;
                        videoActiveTag.get(0).src = rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoLoadIndex].videoBanner;
                    });
                }
                return loadedDef.promise();
            }else if(adframe === "nv-1" || adframe === "nv-2"){
                if(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe].posterBanner && videoActiveTag.get(0).poster.indexOf(videoBlankPoster) == -1) {
                    // 止め絵の表示
                    videoActiveTag.removeClass('is-play');
                    cmBanner.css('visibility', 'hidden');
                    cmSound.css('visibility', 'hidden');
                    videoActiveTag.height(165).width(244);
                    //Safariはポスターセットしたら即ロード
                    videoActiveTag.get(0).poster = rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe].posterBanner ? rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe].posterBanner : videoBlankPoster;
                    videoLink.find("a").attr("href",rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe].nvBannerClickUrl);
                    videoActiveTag.get(0).load();
                    posterDisplay = true;
                }
                loadedDef.resolve();
                return loadedDef.promise();
            }
        }().then( function(){
            // ハンドラの除去
            if (listenerKey !== null) {
                loadedDef = null;
                if(adframe === "sv-1" || adframe === "sv-2"){
                	videoNextTag.get(0).removeEventListener('canplay', listenerKey);
                }
            }
        }),
        stopVideo().then(function(){
            if( loadedDef ) {
                loadedDef.resolve();
                loadedDef = null;
            }
        })
    ).then(function() {
        cmBanner.css('visibility', '');
        cmSound.css('visibility', '');
        videoActiveTag.addClass('is-play');
        videoActiveTag.height(138).width(244);
        if((adframe === "sv-1" || adframe === "sv-2") && (rectangleCM[adframe + "_LENGTH"] > 1)){
            //止め画像ありの動画広告　→　次の動画広告の再生
            if(posterDisplay) {
                if(!(ua.indexOf('chrome') !== -1 && ua.indexOf('edge') == -1)) {
                    videoNextTag.get(0).poster = videoBlankPoster;
                }
                videoActiveTag.hide();
                videoLink.find("a").attr("target",rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].target);
                videoLink.find("a").attr("alt",rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].alt);
                videoLink.find("a").attr("href",rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].clickUrl);
                cmBanner.find("img").attr('src', rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].cmBanner);
                cmBanner.find("a").attr('href', rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoEventIndex].clickUrl);
                if((ua.indexOf('safari')  !== -1 && ua.indexOf('chrome') === -1)) {
                    videoNextTag.fadeIn('slow');
                }else{
                    videoNextTag.show();
                }
                videoNextTag.get(0).play();
                var videoLoadIndex = videoEventIndex + 1 > rectangleCM[adframe + "_LENGTH"] - 1 ? 0  : videoEventIndex + 1;
                videoActiveTag.get(0).src = rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe][videoLoadIndex].videoBanner;
            }
        }else if(rectangleCM[adframe + "_LENGTH"] == 1){
            videoActiveTag.get(0).play();
            videoLink.find("a").attr('href', rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe].clickUrl);
        }else if(adframe === "nv-1" || adframe === "nv-2"){
            videoActiveTag.get(0).play();
            videoLink.find("a").attr('href', rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe].clickUrl);
        }
    });
    function stopVideo() {
        var timeDef = new $.Deferred();
        if(!posterDisplay) {
            timeDef.resolve();
        }else{
            setTimeout(function () {
                timeDef.resolve();
            }, 5000);
        }
        return timeDef.promise();
    }
}

var soundOff ="//p.dmm.com/p/top/bnr/sound_off.gif";

/**
 * 動画と付属バナーのDOMを生成
 * @param ad 広告データ
 * @param adframe 枠の名前
 */
function createRectangleVideoDOM(ad, adframe)
{
	//動画ロード完了前に中心に表示
    var playImg = "//p.dmm.com/p/top/bnr/bt_play.png";

    //指定した枠の一番上の動画広告
    adframe.indexOf("sv") != -1 ? ad = ad[adframe][0] : ad = ad[adframe];


    //付属バナーのありなしでトルツメ
    if(ad.cmBanner){
        var sbRectElement = $("<div></div>", {"class": "sb rect-banner"});
    }else{
        var sbRectElement = $("<div></div>", {"class": "sb rect-banner"});
        sbRectElement.css({'margin-bottom':'-15px'});
    }
    var sbsElement = $("<div></div>", {"class": "sbs"});
    var wrapElement = $("<div></div>", {"class": "wrap-cm"});
    var areaElement = $("<div></div>", {"class": "area-cm"});
    var videoplayElement = $("<div></div>", {"class": "top-cm","id":'top-cm-div-token-'+ adframe, position:'absolute', top:'0', left:'0', width: 244, height: 165});
    var contentsElement = $("<div></div>", {"class": "contents-cm"});
    var videoElement = null;
    var imgElement = null;

    //動画本体のDOM
    var videoLink;
    if(adframe === "sv-1" || adframe === "sv-2") {
        videoLink = $("<a></a>", {href: ad.clickUrl, target: ad.target});
            rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adframe].some(function (ad, index) {
            //生成するvideoタグは1枠につき最大2つ
            //特別枠の'video'タグを作成する。(必要な属性を付与する)
            videoElement = $("<video></video>", {
                src: ad.videoBanner,
                id: "video-" + adframe + "-" + index,
                preload: 'auto',
                muted: true,
                controls: false,
                "class": "is-play",
                alt: ad.alt,
                width: 244,
                height: 138,
                "data-adgroup-id": ad.groupId,
                "data-banner-category": "video",
                "data-order": 1,
                "data-adspace-id": ad.spaceId,
                "data-adspace-name": ad.spaceName
            });
            mousedownForTracking(videoElement.get(0));
            //ポスターバナーのHTMLタグを追加
            imgElement = $("<img></img>", {src: ad.posterBanner, width: '244', height: '165'});
            videoElement.append(imgElement).hide();
            videoLink.append(videoElement);
            if(index == 1) return true
        });
        videoLink.on("contextmenu", function () {return false;});
    }else{
        //通常枠の'video'タグを作成する。(必要な属性を付与する)
        videoElement = $("<video></video>", {
            src: ad.videoBanner,
            id: "video-" + adframe,
            preload: 'auto',
            muted: true,
            controls: false,
            "class": "is-play",
            alt: ad.alt,
            width: 244,
            height: 138,
            "data-adgroup-id": ad.groupId,
            "data-banner-category": "video",
            "data-order": adframe.match(/nv-(\d)/)[1],
            "data-adspace-id": ad.adSpaceId,
            "data-adspace-name": "rectangle_standard"
        });
        mousedownForTracking(videoElement.get(0));
        videoElement.on("contextmenu",function(){return false;});
        //ポスターバナーのHTMLタグを追加
        videoElement.append($("<img></img>", {src: ad.posterBanner, width: '244', height: '165'}));

        //動画本体をURLリンクでラップ
        videoLink = $("<a></a>", {href: ad.clickUrl, target:ad.target});
        videoLink.append(videoElement);
    }

    var movieElement = $("<p></p>", {"class": "movie", "id": "movie-" + adframe});
    movieElement.append(videoLink);

    var soundElement = $("<span></span>", {"class": "cm-sound", "id": "cm-sound-token_" + adframe});
    soundElement.append($("<img></img>", {src: soundOff, width: '62', height: '12'}));
    contentsElement.append(movieElement).append(soundElement);

    //付属バナーのありなしでトルツメ
    if(ad.cmBanner){
        var cmBannerElement = $("<p></p>", {"class": "cm-banner", id: "cm-banner-" + adframe});
        var cmBannerhref;
        if(adframe === "sv-1" || adframe === "sv-2") {
            //付属バナー要素の作成
            cmBannerhref = $("<a></a>", {href: ad.clickUrl, target: ad.target, "data-adgroup-id": ad.groupId, "data-banner-category": "footer","data-adspace-id": ad.spaceId, "data-adspace-name": ad.spaceName})
              .append($('<img />', {src: ad.cmBanner, width: 244, height: 27}));
            mousedownForTracking(cmBannerhref.get(0));
        }else{
            //付属バナー要素の作成
            cmBannerhref = $("<a></a>", {href: ad.nvBannerClickUrl, target: ad.target,"data-order": adframe.match(/nv-(\d)/)[1], "data-adgroup-id": ad.groupId, "data-banner-category": "footer","data-adspace-id": ad.footerAdSpaceId, "data-adspace-name": "rectangle_standard_video_attachment"})
	          .append($('<img />', {src: ad.cmBanner, width: 244, height: 27}));
            mousedownForTracking(cmBannerhref.get(0));
        }
        cmBannerElement.append(cmBannerhref);
        areaElement.append(contentsElement).append(cmBannerElement);
    }else{
        areaElement.append(contentsElement);
    }

    var playElement =$("<p></p>").append($('<img />', {src: playImg, width: 50, height: 104, alt:""}));
    videoplayElement.append(playElement);
    wrapElement.append(areaElement);
    wrapElement.append(videoplayElement);

    sbsElement.append(wrapElement);
    sbRectElement.append(sbsElement);

    //ビデオタグ各種のイベントハンドラの設定
    //動画の再生
    videoplayElement.click(function(){
        videoLink.children('video:visible').get(0).play();
        videoplayElement.css('visibility', 'hidden');
        soundElement.find("img").css('visibility', '');
    });

    //音声ミュート
    soundElement.click(function () {
        videoLink.children().each(function(index, video){
            video.muted = !video.muted;
            video.defaultMuted = video.muted;
        });
        //ミュート状態で画像を差し替え
        var fn = 'sound_on.gif';
        if (videoElement.get(0).muted) {
            fn = 'sound_off.gif';
        }
        $(this).find('img').attr('src', 'https://p.dmm.com/p/top/bnr/' + fn);
    });
    soundElement.hover(
        function () {
            $(this).css("cursor", "pointer");
        },
        function () {
            $(this).css("cursor", "default");
        }
    );

    return sbRectElement;
}

//サーバー、ネットワーク障害発生時に代替広告を表示
function insertAlternateRightAd()
{
    try {
        if (isRightAd) return;

        var alternateAd = new Object();
        alternateAd.creative = new Object();
        alternateAd.creative.source = "//p.dmm.com/p/bnr/ad/right/netgame01_g.jpg";
        alternateAd.clickUrl = "http://ad.dmm.com/ad/p/r?_site=242&_article=9743&_link=258294&_image=258384";
        var adElement = createRightBanner(alternateAd);

        //バックフィル通常 枠を設定する
        adElement.dataset.order = 1;
        adElement.dataset.adspaceName = "rectangle_standard";
        adElement.dataset.adspaceId = "0";
        adElement.dataset.adgroupId = "0";

        if (adElement && $("#right-ad-container").is(":empty")) {

            //広告枠が空であれば代替広告をセット
            $("#right-ad-container").append(adElement);
            isRightAd = true;

            //効果測定
            ga('mutual.send', 'event', 'backfill_mk', 'top', 'rectangle', {nonInteraction: true});

            mousedownForTracking(adElement);
        }
    } catch (e) {
        //何もしない
    }
}
//サーバー、ネットワーク障害発生時に特別枠の動画広告を表示
function insertAlternateRightSpecialVideoAd(){
    if(isRightSpecialVideoAd1 && isRightSpecialVideoAd2) return;
    try {
        //ini設定のバックフィル動画セット
        if(Object.keys(rectangleCM["BACKFILL_MOVIE_DATA"]).length === 0){
            rectangleCM["BACKFILL_MOVIE_DATA"] = JSON.parse('[]');
        }
        //特別動画枠①
        if (!isRightSpecialVideoAd1) {
            adFrame = "sv-1";
            isRightSpecialVideoAd1 = true;
            rectangleCM.createRectangleCmBackFillMovie(rectangleCM["BACKFILL_MOVIE_DATA"], adFrame);

            if (rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adFrame]) {
                if (rectangleCM.checkRectangleCmMovieFormat(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adFrame])) {
                    $("#right-ad-container").prepend(createRectangleVideoDOM(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"], adFrame));
                    setEventCM(adFrame);
                } else {
                    //バックフィルの設定が不十分だったら描画しない
                }
            }
        }
        //特別動画枠②
        if(!isRightSpecialVideoAd2){
            adFrame = "sv-2";
            isRightSpecialVideoAd2 = true;
            rectangleCM.createRectangleCmBackFillMovie(rectangleCM["BACKFILL_MOVIE_DATA"], adFrame);
            if (rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adFrame]) {
                if (rectangleCM.checkRectangleCmMovieFormat(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"][adFrame])) {
                    //CM特別動画枠②はCM特別枠①の下部に配置する
                    if ($("#video-sv-1-0").length === 0) {
                        $("#right-ad-container").prepend(createRectangleVideoDOM(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"], adFrame));
                    } else {
                        $("#right-ad-container").children().eq(0).after(createRectangleVideoDOM(rectangleCM["MOVIE_DATA"], adFrame));
                    }
                    setEventCM(adFrame);
                } else {
                    //バックフィルの設定が不十分だったら描画しない
                }
            }
        }
    } catch (e) {
        //何もしない
    }
}
function mousedownForTracking(element) {
    if (document.addEventListener) {
        element.addEventListener("mousedown", clickTrackingDisplayAd, false);
    } else if ( document.readyState === "complete" ) {
    	element.addEventListener("onmousedown", clickTrackingDisplayAd);
    }
}
/**
 * アドサーバクリック時の情報を送信
 * 2019/02/12 時点では`pigeon`へ送信
 */
function clickTrackingDisplayAd()
{
    try{
        /**
         * クリック時のアンカータグ独自属性に トラッキング情報を持たせておく。
         * 独自属性を取得し、ライブラリへ渡す。トラッキング送信自体はライブラリ内で行う。
         * その他の属性以外は、ライブラリ側で補完する
         */
        // ad_space_nameの取得 adspaceIdがなければ、backfillとする。
        var ad_space_name = $(this).data('adspaceId') ? $(this).data('adspaceName') : $(this).data('adspaceName') + "_backfill";
        // ページの見た目で判定を行う。(ユーザエージェントでは行わない)
        var view_type = document.getElementById("i3_vwtp").value || "";

        //JQueryに依存するパラメータを取得する
        var parameter = {
            "environment" : phpParam.isDev ? "stage":"production",
            "ad_space_name" : ad_space_name,
            "ad_space_id" : $(this).data('adspaceId'),
            "ad_group_id" : $(this).data('adgroupId'),
            "ad_order" : $(this).data('order') || 1,
            "site_type" : phpParam.isAdult ? "adult":"general",
            "view_type" : view_type
        };

        // Pigeonの仮URLに送信
        var displayad = new adtech_mkbase.displayad.DisplayadTracking();
        displayad.sendTrackingBeacon("/marketing_ad/click/displayad", parameter);
    }catch (e) {
        //adtech_mkbase.displayad.DisplayadTracking がうまく読み込めないなどのエラーの場合は何も行わない
    }
}
